< Rating>
4</Rating>
< text>
Have had my eyes on this place for some time! Was pretty excited to see they had finally opened. First impression was the decor was pretty nice, the wall artwork definitely catches the eye. The menu is pretty expansive, even offering chicken wings (which weren't half bad.) I went with the "Good Ol Burger", which was pretty tasty. The beef is certainly of good quality, and the toasted brioche bun had the right amount of bite to it. The french fries left something to be desired, and the portion could have been larger, but they were hot and fresh with the right amount of salt so no real complaints there. Cost is a little high for the area, but for the quality of ingredients is more than acceptable. I will definitely be returning in the future.
PROS: Good quality for the price, food is fresh and tasty, diverse offerings without feeling hipster
CONS: Could have been more generous with the fries, for a place with "cheese" in the name the cheese plate offerings weren't much
OVERALL: I would definitely recommend this place. Nice to have a proper burger joint in Clairemont.<//text>

This Review has been Edited to reflect the business and Idotechs great customer service

(Before) I got a screen replacement for my iphone 8 Plus, I paid 80$ and was assured that it would be a great quality however, they blatantly lied. My phone fell about 2 feet off my bed with a case AND a screen protector on and the screen cracked. A noticeable crack straight across the top and two straight down. Want to know how I can tell how cheap this is? My screen protector is completely fine with no cracks! How did the phone break and not the screen protector?! This is one of the cheapest screens they could probably get and straight up lied to me. My phone lasted a week and half with this screen, I will demand a refund once they open.

EDIT: Current Review
After writing this review and calling them they responded immediately and asked me to go to their shop to see what they can do for me. I went in a month after because I am still unable to drive and live a bit far from this place so I am very thankful that they even considered replacing the screen again. Although they did not do it for free they offered me a 50% discount so I payed 40$ to have the screen replaced again. These guys have great customer service and I appreciate them for offering anything whereas other places would probably not do anything. Although I am still unsure of the quality of the screen the phone looks and feels like new I just hope it doesn‚Äôt break again so easily or soon.I also want to say thanks and ultimately recommend this place to anyone looking to fix their electronics.

< Text>
Voted best in OC and I can taste why. This is the second location located adjacent to Rodeo 39 right outside the big door way.

You order and pay at the door then seat yourself (at least we did because we sat outside, maybe they seat you if you sit indoor).

Everything on the menu is $10. Super cheap and authentic quality. Usually oxtail would be extra but all 16 items is $10 each. You get a choice of large or small noodles. Go with the small, it‚Äôs less starchy and filling.

A plate of veggie herbs came out, plate bean sprouts and extra onions. Along with sriracha and hoisin each in a two ounce cup.

The pho is served in a metal bowl. I took a sip of the broth and at first, it was salty but that‚Äôs before I mixed it or added limes. After I did, the bone broth was flavorful. Everything came together.

Most importantly is MSG, we are very sensitive and stop eating at places that uses MSG. We didn‚Äôt taste any here or it‚Äôs very light which is a plus.< /Text>

<text>Well, what can I say. We were greeted by the entryway and were advised that there was a 30 minute wait, and that we had to wait outside until we got a text. We went inside to get something to drink and noticed lots of tables available in the bar.Hmmm. Yet we were told  we couldn't have a drink in the bar. Anyways,  we were asked by the front desk if we were waiting and they proceeded to seat us immediately.  Our waiter Stefan was most courteous and took our drink requests.  We got our drinks and ordered some tumbleweeds for the appetizers,  these are the best onion ring extraordinaire.  We ordered Dakota Chicken with bacon, mushrooms,  and a honey mustard sauce. My sister had the New York steak, which came out perfectly cooked. I ordered the Salmon, blackened with baked potatoes all around. Your bread is the best...with the soft dough in the center, and so hearty crust. Tastes so good with lots of good butter. What makes this even better than most other places is that the butter comes soft, ready to smooth on the bread....not tearing up the bread. We enjoyed our meals as always, and left a hearty tip for our waiter. He really enjoys his job, which goes a long way during these times. We try to stop at Cattleman's whenever we come across one in our travels. < Review>
Husband and I went for my birthday. The second we walked in, we were seated.  As soon as we were seated they placed warm bread and butter on our table.  We skipped the appetizers and ordered our dinner. I ordered the steak and shrimp.  He ordered Pete's Special.  Our meals came with all you can eat salad, our choice of side, and beans.  We must of been having a great time. It only seemed like minutes after we ordered that we got our meal.  Every item that was ordered was delicious! It was one of the most satisfying meals we had in a long time.  The service was great.  The atmosphere is country cozy.  Definitely a place we will be visiting again.< /Review>

In our party we had my parents both retired snd over 55, my wife and I both in our late twenties and early 30s and a 12 year old child. There was choices for everyone. My wife and I loved our meal although my wifes steak was medium well and she ordered well done, the steaks had great flavor. The child enjoyed his food, my mothers steak salad was not impressive to her, she felt the meat was too tough. My father over all liked his steak but felt it had to much fat on it. Deserts were all great, the  new york cheesecake is great, about 4 inches thick and very fluffy. Over all a great dinning experience. Had everyone in my party been impressed i would have rated 5 stars.<//review>

<Text>We recently celebrated our mother's 70th birthday here. While the servers were very polite, they obviously don't have the staff to handle the crowd they get. We were sat in the corner of very back room(there were 11 of us). I am disabled, but I was able to squeeze in between the wall and table.
Our drink & appetizer orders were promptly taken, but I was never offered a refill the entire time (though my brother who was sitting right next to me was offered one, even though my cup was empty and his was half full). I figured I'd ask for a refill when she brought his back, but she pretended to not hear me when I started talking to her. I guess the eye contact and my moving lips threw her for a loop.
The chicken I bought was rubbery and not worth the price at all.  The mashed potatoes were dry and chock-full of very stale chives or green onions that was like chewing cud.
Thankfully my mother appeared to be enjoying her meal, and never needed a refill or any extras.
I also asked two seperate servers for a straw and never received one(even though I later noticed most servers had them in their apron).
All in all, it seems I was ignored because I was sitting at the end of the table, and therefore an inconvenience for the servers to bother paying attention to.
I didn't complain because I wanted my mom to have the perfect day, and she was having a good time(though she later told me her steak was very tough). But my brothers noticed the staff ignoring me, as did the family at the neighboring table. They even apologized to me because they felt bad(the family, not the servers).
